 TERI University is investing in regional water studies
 bataa rahe hai jayant shriramani dilli kii tiiarai uniwarsity ne sastenebel deveopment kii field main thot leadership nirmaan centre ke rup main apni pahchaan banaai he
 This year it has partnered with the coca-cola Foundation to bridge the gap in India's water resources management sector
 jal sansadhano kaa prabhavi istemaal or sangrakshan bharat ke liye ek ahm masalaa ho saktaa he lekin long turm planning ke maamle main yahaan trend logon kii baari kami he
 In 2012, the Central Water Resources Department released the National Water Policy, calling it an area of concern and stating that due to lack of trained professionals in scientific planning, use of modern technologies and analytical capabilities, good water management We are untouched
 isamen water management kii disha main samgr soch na hone kii ore bhi ishaara kiya gaya tha or kaha gaya ki sarkari agenciyon kii vajah se hi jal se jude masalon par sambandhit logon se baat nahin kii jaati he or akasar iske nattejey kharaab or bharose laayak seva na milane ke rup main saamne aate hai
 To overcome this deficiency, TERI University has established the coca-cola Department of Regional Water Studies in association with the coca-cola Foundation
 department interdiciplinary fremawork ke tahat vibhinn pahaluon kaa akalan kar rahaa he jo saanskrithik, shaikshanik or vaigyanik karkon ke saath hi dharmik, jaateey, saamaajik, rajnatik, kanoonee, sansthagat or aarthik pahaluon ko dhyaan main rakhkar water management ke bare main aage kii raah taiyaar karegaa
